class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="introduction"><a data-card="" href="#introduction" class="peer">Introduction</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>In this comprehensive vibe coding tutorial, you&#x27;ll build a complete <strong>Linktree clone SaaS</strong> application from scratch using AI assistance. This guide teaches you how to leverage AI tools to rapidly develop a full-stack application with:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong><a href="https://nextjs.org/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Next.js</a></strong> — React framework for production</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.prisma.io/orm" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Prisma ORM</a></strong> — Type-safe database access</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.prisma.io/postgres" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Prisma Postgres</a></strong> — Serverless PostgreSQL database</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://clerk.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Clerk</a></strong> — Authentication and user management</li>
</ul>
<p>By the end of this tutorial, you&#x27;ll have a working SaaS application where users can sign up, create their profile, and manage their personal link page — all built with AI-assisted development.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">What is Vibe Coding?<p>Vibe coding is a development approach where you collaborate with AI assistants to build applications. You describe what you want to build, and the AI helps generate the code while you guide the direction and make architectural decisions.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="video-tutorial"><a data-card="" href="#video-tutorial" class="peer">Video tutorial</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Watch this step-by-step walkthrough of the entire build process:</p>
<div class="videoWrapper"><iframe width="560" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/R3GJ1eo943k" title="YouTube video player" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture"></iframe></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="prerequisites"><a data-card="" href="#prerequisites" class="peer">Prerequisites</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Before starting this tutorial, make sure you have:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://nodejs.org" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Node.js 20+</a> installed</li>
<li>A <a href="https://clerk.com" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Clerk account</a> (free tier works)</li>
<li>An AI coding assistant (<a href="https://cursor.com" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Cursor</a>, <a href="https://windsurf.com" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Windsurf</a>, <a href="https://github.com/features/copilot" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">GitHub Copilot</a>, etc.)</li>
<li>Basic familiarity with React and TypeScript</li>
</ul>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">Recommended AI Models<p>For best results, we recommend using the latest AI models such as (minimum) Claude Sonnet 4, Gemini 2.5 Pro, or GPT-4o. These models provide better code generation accuracy and understand complex architectural patterns.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="1-set-up-your-project"><a data-card="" href="#1-set-up-your-project" class="peer">1. Set Up Your Project</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Let&#x27;s start by creating a new Next.js application:</p>

<p>Once the setup is complete, you&#x27;ll need to add <strong>Prisma</strong> and <strong>Prisma Postgres</strong> to your project. We&#x27;ve prepared a detailed prompt that handles the complete setup for you.</p>
<p>👉 <strong>Find the setup prompt here:</strong> <a href="/docs/ai/prompts/nextjs">Next.js + Prisma Prompt</a></p>
<p><strong>How to use it:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>Create a new file called <code>prompt.md</code> at the root of your project</li>
<li>Copy and paste the prompt content into this file</li>
<li>Ask your AI assistant to follow the instructions in this file</li>
</ol>
<p>The AI will set up Prisma ORM, create your database connection, and configure everything automatically.</p>

<p>If both commands run without errors and you can see sample data in Prisma Studio, you&#x27;re ready to continue!</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">Good Practice: Commit Early and Often<p>Throughout this tutorial, we&#x27;ll commit our changes regularly. This makes it easy to track progress and roll back if something goes wrong.</p><p>Start by linking your project to GitHub:</p><figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> init</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> .</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> commit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -m</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Initial setup: Next.js app with Prisma&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="2-set-up-authentication-with-clerk"><a data-card="" href="#2-set-up-authentication-with-clerk" class="peer">2. Set Up Authentication with Clerk</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Now let&#x27;s add user authentication using <a href="https://clerk.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Clerk</a>, which provides a complete authentication solution out of the box.</p>
<p><strong>Steps to follow:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>Go to <a href="https://clerk.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Clerk</a> and create an account (if you don&#x27;t have one)</li>
<li>Create a new application in your Clerk dashboard</li>
<li>Follow Clerk&#x27;s official quickstart guide to integrate it with your Next.js app:</li>
</ol>
<p>👉 <strong>Clerk Next.js Quickstart:</strong> <a href="https://clerk.com/docs/nextjs/getting-started/quickstart" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">clerk.com/docs/nextjs/getting-started/quickstart</a></p>
<p>The guide will walk you through installing the SDK, adding environment variables, and wrapping your app with the <code>ClerkProvider</code>.</p>
<p>Once complete, commit your changes:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> .</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> commit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -m</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Add Clerk authentication setup&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="3-update-your-database-schema"><a data-card="" href="#3-update-your-database-schema" class="peer">3. Update Your Database Schema</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Since we&#x27;re building a Linktree clone, we need to update the database schema to support our specific data model. This includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>A <code>User</code> model with a unique <code>username</code> (for public profile URLs like <code>/username</code>)</li>
<li>A <code>Link</code> model to store each user&#x27;s links</li>
</ul>
<p>Replace the contents of your <code>prisma/schema.prisma</code> file with the following:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">prisma/schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">generator</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> client</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../app/generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">datasource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> db</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Example User model for testing</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">      @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">autoincrement</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  username  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> // Important for the public profile URL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  clerkId   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> // Links to Clerk Auth</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name      </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  links     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Link</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">now</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  updatedAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @updatedAt</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Link</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">      @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">autoincrement</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  url       </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  userId    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  user      </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">     @relation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">fields</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">userId</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">references</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">now</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Since we&#x27;re changing the schema structure, we need to reset the database. The existing seed data was just for testing purposes, so it&#x27;s safe to drop and recreate:</p>

aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> db</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> push</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --force-reset</span></span></code></pre></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_17p7lfivpfiv9db_-trigger-pnpm" hidden="" id="radix-_R_17p7lfivpfiv9db_-content-pnpm" tabindex="0"></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_17p7lfivpfiv9db_-trigger-yarn" hidden="" id="radix-_R_17p7lfivpfiv9db_-content-yarn" tabindex="0"></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_17p7lfivpfiv9db_-trigger-bun" hidden="" id="radix-_R_17p7lfivpfiv9db_-content-bun" tabindex="0"></div></div>
<p>This command:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Drops</strong> the existing database tables</li>
<li><strong>Creates</strong> new tables based on your updated schema</li>
</ul>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-warning border-none text-foreground-warning [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-warning"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">Use with Caution<p>The <code>--force-reset</code> flag deletes all existing data. This is fine during prototyping, but never use it on a production database! Once your schema is stable, switch to <code>prisma migrate dev</code> for proper migration tracking.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-1"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-1" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Open Prisma Studio to verify the new schema is applied:</p>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="bg-background-default rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral overflow-hidden my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal" <p>You should see the updated <code>User</code> and <code>Link</code> tables (they&#x27;ll be empty, which is expected).</p>
<p><strong>Commit your changes:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> .</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> commit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -m</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Update schema for Linktree clone&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="4-connect-clerk-users-to-your-database"><a data-card="" href="#4-connect-clerk-users-to-your-database" class="peer">4. Connect Clerk Users to Your Database</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Here&#x27;s the challenge: when a user signs in with Clerk, they exist in Clerk&#x27;s system but <strong>not</strong> in your database. We need to bridge this gap.</p>
<p>Our approach: create a &quot;Claim Username&quot; flow where users pick their unique username (e.g., <code>yourapp.com/johndoe</code>) after signing in for the first time.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">Use ASK Mode First<p>When working with AI assistants, we recommend using <strong>ASK mode</strong> by default to review suggested changes before applying them. Only switch to AGENT mode once you&#x27;re comfortable with the proposed code.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="the-prompt"><a data-card="" href="#the-prompt" class="peer">The Prompt</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Copy and paste the following prompt into your AI assistant:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Connect Clerk authentication to your Prisma database with a &quot;Claim Username&quot; flow.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Goal:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">When a user signs in via Clerk, they don&#x27;t automatically exist in YOUR database. Create a flow where:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Logged out → Show landing page with &quot;Sign In&quot; button</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Logged in but no DB profile → Show &quot;Claim Username&quot; form</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Has DB profile → Show dashboard</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**User Model (already in schema):**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model User {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">id Int @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">email String @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">username String @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">clerkId String @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">name String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">links Link[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">createdAt DateTime @default(now())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Files to create/update:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `app/actions.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> - Server Action with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`claimUsername(formData)`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `app/page.tsx`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> - Three-state UI (logged out / claim username / dashboard)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `app/api/users/route.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> - Update POST to accept </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`clerkId`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`email`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`username`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`name`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;use server&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> directive in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`app/actions.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`currentUser()`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@clerk/nextjs/server`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to get auth user</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Store </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`clerkId`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`email`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`username`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`name`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in User model</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`redirect(&quot;/&quot;)`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> after successful profile creation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Handle username uniqueness (Prisma will throw if duplicate)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Server Action receives FormData, validates username (min 3 chars, alphanumeric + underscore)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Creates User in Prisma with Clerk&#x27;s </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`user.id`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`clerkId`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Page.tsx checks: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`currentUser()`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → then </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { clerkId } })`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Render different UI based on auth state and DB state</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Keep it simple:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No middleware file needed</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No webhook sync (user creates profile manually)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Basic validation (username length &gt;= 3)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Errors just throw (no fancy error UI for MVP)</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>After the AI generates the code, you may see TypeScript errors. This is because the Prisma Client needs to be regenerated to reflect the schema changes:</p>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-2"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-2" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Test the complete flow:</p>
<ol>
<li>Stop your dev server and restart it</li>
<li>Open your app in the browser</li>
<li>Sign up as a new user through Clerk</li>
<li>You should see the &quot;Claim Username&quot; form</li>
<li>Enter a username and submit</li>
<li>Verify the user appears in Prisma Studio (<code>npm run db:studio</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>If everything works, commit your changes!</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="5-upgrade-the-ui-design"><a data-card="" href="#5-upgrade-the-ui-design" class="peer">5. Upgrade the UI Design</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Let&#x27;s give our app a more polished, friendly look inspired by platforms like Buy Me a Coffee.</p>
<p>👉 <a href="https://buymeacoffee.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Visit Buy Me a Coffee for design inspiration</a></p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt to your AI assistant:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Design a minimal, friendly UI inspired by Buy Me a Coffee.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Theme:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Force light mode only (no dark mode switching)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Clean white background (#FFFFFF)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Black text (#000000) for headings</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Gray (#6B7280) for secondary text</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Bright yellow (#FFDD00) for CTA buttons</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Light gray (#F7F7F7) for cards/sections</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Subtle borders (#E5E5E5)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Typography &amp; Spacing:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Large, bold headlines (text-5xl or bigger)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Generous whitespace and padding</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Rounded corners everywhere (rounded-full for buttons, rounded-xl for cards)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Buttons:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Primary: Yellow background, black text, rounded-full, font-semibold</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Secondary: White background, border, rounded-full</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Overall feel:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Friendly, approachable, not corporate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Minimal — only essential elements</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Mobile-first with good touch targets (py-4, px-8 on buttons)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> One unified canvas — background applies to the entire page (body), with white cards floating on top. No separate section backgrounds.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Use Tailwind CSS. Keep it simple.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-3"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-3" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>After the AI applies the changes:</p>
<ol>
<li>Refresh your app and browse through all pages</li>
<li>Verify the design has updated but <strong>no functionality has changed</strong></li>
<li>Test the sign-in flow and username claim process</li>
</ol>
<p>Once verified, commit the changes:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> .</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">git</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> commit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -m</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Update UI design&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="6-build-link-management-add--delete"><a data-card="" href="#6-build-link-management-add--delete" class="peer">6. Build Link Management (Add &amp; Delete)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Now let&#x27;s add the core functionality: managing links! Users should be able to add new links and delete existing ones from their dashboard.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Build a simple dashboard for managing links using Next.js App Router and Server Actions.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Server Component page that fetches user data from database</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;Add Link&quot; form with Title and URL inputs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> List of existing links with Delete button</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use Server Actions (no API routes) for create/delete operations</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`revalidatePath(&quot;/&quot;)`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> after mutations to refresh the page</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create server actions in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`actions.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;use server&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> directive</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Pass actions directly to form </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`action`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prop</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Keep page.tsx as a Server Component (no &#x27;use client&#x27;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use hidden inputs for IDs (e.g., </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&lt;input type=&quot;hidden&quot; name=&quot;linkId&quot; value={id} /&gt;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Keep it simple:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No loading states</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No client components</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No confirmation dialogs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Just forms + server actions + revalidation</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This is the MVP pattern for CRUD with Next.js App Router.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-4"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-4" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Test the link management:</p>
<ol>
<li>Add a new link with a title and URL</li>
<li>Verify it appears in your dashboard</li>
<li>Delete the link</li>
<li>Verify it&#x27;s removed</li>
</ol>
<p>Both operations should work instantly without page navigation.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="7-create-public-profile-pages"><a data-card="" href="#7-create-public-profile-pages" class="peer">7. Create Public Profile Pages</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>This is the heart of a Linktree clone: public profile pages that anyone can visit at <code>/username</code>.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Build a public profile page at /[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">username</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">] using Next.js App Router dynamic routes.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`app/[username]/page.tsx`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as a Server Component</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Fetch user + links from database by username (from URL params)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Return 404 if user not found (use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`notFound()`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> from next/navigation)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Display: avatar (first letter), username, name, and list of links</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Links open in new tab with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`target=&quot;_blank&quot;`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Add a small &quot;Create your own&quot; link at the bottom</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Get params: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`const { username } = await params`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Query database with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`findUnique({ where: { username } })`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If no user: call </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`notFound()`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Render profile with links as clickable buttons</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Keep it simple:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No auth required (it&#x27;s a public page)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Pure Server Component (no &#x27;use client&#x27;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Basic styling with hover effects</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This is the core &quot;Linktree&quot; feature — anyone can visit /username to see the links.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-5"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-5" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Test your public profile:</p>
<ol>
<li>Navigate to <code>localhost:3000/your-username</code> (replace with your actual username)</li>
<li>Verify your profile and links display correctly</li>
<li>Click a link and confirm it opens in a new tab</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="8-add-a-copy-link-button"><a data-card="" href="#8-add-a-copy-link-button" class="peer">8. Add a &quot;Copy Link&quot; Button</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Make it easy for users to share their profile URL with a one-click copy button.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create a Client Component (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;use client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) for the button</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`navigator.clipboard.writeText(url)`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to copy</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Show &quot;Copied!&quot; feedback for 2 seconds after clicking</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`useState`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to toggle the button text</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`app/components/copy-button.tsx`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with &#x27;use client&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Accept </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`url`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as a prop</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> On click: copy to clipboard, set </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`copied`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to true</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`setTimeout`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to reset after 2 seconds</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Import and use in your Server Component page</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Keep it simple:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> One small client component</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No toast libraries</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Just inline text feedback (&quot;Copy link&quot; → &quot;Copied!&quot;)</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-6"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-6" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ol>
<li>Find the &quot;Copy link&quot; button on your dashboard</li>
<li>Click it and verify it shows &quot;Copied!&quot;</li>
<li>Paste somewhere to confirm the URL was copied correctly</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="9-create-a-custom-404-page"><a data-card="" href="#9-create-a-custom-404-page" class="peer">9. Create a Custom 404 Page</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>When someone visits a non-existent username, they should see a friendly error page instead of a generic 404.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Create a custom 404 page for Next.js App Router.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`app/not-found.tsx`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (Server Component)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Display: 404 heading, friendly message, &quot;Go home&quot; button</span></span>
