<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Match your app&#x27;s design (colors, fonts, spacing)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Next.js automatically uses </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`not-found.tsx`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> when </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`notFound()`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> is called</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Or when a route doesn&#x27;t exist</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No configuration needed — just create the file</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Keep it simple:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Static page, no data fetching</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> One heading, one message, one link</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Same styling as rest of the app</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-7"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-7" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Test the 404 page by visiting a random URL like <code>/this-user-does-not-exist</code>. You should see your custom 404 page with a link back to the homepage.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="10-add-a-custom-background"><a data-card="" href="#10-add-a-custom-background" class="peer">10. Add a Custom Background</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Let&#x27;s make the app more visually distinctive with a custom background pattern.</p>
<p><strong>First</strong>, either:</p>
<ul>
<li>Download a background SVG pattern you like, or</li>
<li>Create your own using tools like <a href="https://www.svgbackgrounds.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">SVG Backgrounds</a> or <a href="https://heropatterns.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Hero Patterns</a></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Then</strong>, save it as <code>background.svg</code> in your <code>public/</code> folder.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Add a custom SVG background to my app.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> The svg file is in the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`public/`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> folder (e.g., </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`public/background.svg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Apply it as a fixed, full-cover background on the body</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">In </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`globals.css`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, update the body:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```css</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">body {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  background: var(--background) url(&quot;/background.svg&quot;) center/cover no-repeat fixed;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  min-height: 100vh;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Key properties:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `center/cover`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — centers and scales to fill</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `no-repeat`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — prevents tiling</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `fixed`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — background stays in place when scrolling</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Files in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`public/`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> are served at the root URL, so </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`/background.svg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> works.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-8"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-8" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ol>
<li>Refresh your app</li>
<li>Verify the background appears on <strong>all pages</strong> (homepage, dashboard, profile pages, 404)</li>
<li>If the background doesn&#x27;t appear everywhere, ask your AI to fix it</li>
</ol>
<p>Commit your changes once it&#x27;s working correctly.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="11-add-glassmorphism-card-containers"><a data-card="" href="#11-add-glassmorphism-card-containers" class="peer">11. Add Glassmorphism Card Containers</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Create visual depth by adding semi-transparent card containers that &quot;float&quot; over the background.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Add a reusable card container class to create visual separation from the background.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Requirements:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create a </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.card`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> class in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`globals.css`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Apply glassmorphism: semi-transparent white + blur</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use on all main content areas (landing, forms, dashboard, profile pages)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">In </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`globals.css`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, add:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```css</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.card {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  backdrop-filter: blur(10px);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  border-radius: 1.5rem;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  padding: 2rem;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  box-shadow: 0 4px 24px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Usage:**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Wrap content sections with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&lt;div className=&quot;card&quot;&gt;...&lt;/div&gt;`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">For public profile pages (/[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">username</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Wrap the entire profile (avatar, name, username, and links list) in a single .card container</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This creates a Linktree-style floating card effect</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Footer/attribution links stay outside the card</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Hero section:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Add a soft radial glow behind the content (large blurred white circle, blur-3xl, 50% opacity)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">No visible container edges — just organic, fading brightness</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Content floats freely over the glow</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Result:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Content &quot;lifts&quot; off the background</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Subtle blur creates depth</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Consistent UI across all pages</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="12-display-clerk-profile-images"><a data-card="" href="#12-display-clerk-profile-images" class="peer">12. Display Clerk Profile Images</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>If users sign in with Google or another OAuth provider, Clerk stores their profile photo. Let&#x27;s display it on public profiles!</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">On the public profile page (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`/[username]`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">), display the user&#x27;s Clerk profile image (Google photo, etc.) instead of the initial letter avatar.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Pattern:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Fetch Clerk user to get profile image</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> client</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> clerkClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> clerkUser</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> client.users.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">getUser</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(user.clerkId);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Display:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use a plain </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&lt;img&gt;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> tag (not Next.js Image component)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`clerkUser.imageUrl`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> exists, show the image</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Otherwise fallback to the yellow initial avatar</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Keep it simple:**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No try/catch — let errors bubble up</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No next.config changes needed</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> No database schema changes needed</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-9"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-9" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Visit your public profile page and verify your profile image (from Google, GitHub, etc.) is displayed instead of the initial letter avatar.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="13-add-icons-with-lucide"><a data-card="" href="#13-add-icons-with-lucide" class="peer">13. Add Icons with Lucide</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Small icons can significantly improve UI clarity. Let&#x27;s add some using Lucide React.</p>
<p>Copy and paste this prompt:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Add Lucide React icons to improve the UI.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">First install: npm install lucide-react</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Add icons to these elements:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> View button: ExternalLink icon</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Delete button: Trash2 icon (replace text with icon)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Empty links state: Link icon</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Import icons from &#x27;lucide-react&#x27; and use with size prop (e.g., size={18}).</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Keep buttons minimal — only add icons where they improve clarity.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="quick-check-10"><a data-card="" href="#quick-check-10" class="peer">Quick Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Browse through your app and verify the icons appear on:</p>
<ul>
<li>The view/external link buttons</li>
<li>The delete buttons</li>
<li>The empty state when no links exist</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="14-deploy-to-vercel"><a data-card="" href="#14-deploy-to-vercel" class="peer">14. Deploy to Vercel</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Time to ship! Let&#x27;s deploy your app to Vercel.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-warning border-none text-foreground-warning [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-warning"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">Important Steps<p>Follow these steps carefully to avoid deployment errors.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="step-1-configure-prisma-for-production"><a data-card="" href="#step-1-configure-prisma-for-production" class="peer">Step 1: Configure Prisma for Production</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Add a <code>postinstall</code> script to ensure Prisma Client is generated during deployment.</p>
<p>Add this to your <code>package.json</code> scripts section:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M 6,1 C 4.354992,1 3,2.354992 3,4 v 16 c 0,1.645008 1.354992,3 3,3 h 12 c 1.645008,0 3,-1.354992 3,-3 V 8 7 A 1.0001,1.0001 0 0 0 20.707031,6.2929687 l -5,-5 A 1.0001,1.0001 0 0 0 15,1 h -1 z m 0,2 h 7 v 3 c 0,1.645008 1.354992,3 3,3 h 3 v 11 c 0,0.564129 -0.435871,1 -1,1 H 6 C 5.4358712,21 5,20.564129 5,20 V 4 C 5,3.4358712 5.4358712,3 6,3 Z M 15,3.4140625 18.585937,7 H 16 C 15.435871,7 15,6.5641288 15,6 Z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">package.json</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;scripts&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;postinstall&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma generate&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>📖 <strong>Reference:</strong> <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-client/deployment/serverless/deploy-to-vercel#build-configuration">Deploy to Vercel - Build Configuration</a></p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="step-2-clean-up-development-files"><a data-card="" href="#step-2-clean-up-development-files" class="peer">Step 2: Clean Up Development Files</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Delete the <code>scripts/</code> folder if it exists. This folder was auto-generated during initial setup for seed data, you don&#x27;t need it in production.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="step-3-deploy-to-vercel"><a data-card="" href="#step-3-deploy-to-vercel" class="peer">Step 3: Deploy to Vercel</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ol>
<li>Push your code to GitHub (if you haven&#x27;t already)</li>
<li>Go to <a href="https://vercel.com" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">vercel.com</a> and import your repository</li>
<li><strong>Important:</strong> Add all your environment variables in Vercel&#x27;s dashboard:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>DATABASE_URL</code></li>
<li><code>NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY</code></li>
<li><code>CLERK_SECRET_KEY</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="step-4-update-the-app-url"><a data-card="" href="#step-4-update-the-app-url" class="peer">Step 4: Update the App URL</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>After your first deployment:</p>
<ol>
<li>Copy your production URL from Vercel (e.g., <code>https://your-app.vercel.app</code>)</li>
<li>Add a new environment variable in Vercel:<!-- -->
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL=https://your-app.vercel.app</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
</li>
<li>Redeploy to apply the change</li>
</ol>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-warning border-none text-foreground-warning [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-warning"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit">Don&#x27;t Forget This Step<p>If you skip setting <code>NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL</code>, features like the &quot;Copy Link&quot; button will copy <code>localhost</code> URLs instead of your production URL.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="final-check"><a data-card="" href="#final-check" class="peer">Final Check</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Test your deployed app thoroughly:</p>
<ul class="contains-task-list">
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" class="flex h-9 w-full rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral bg-background-default px-3 py-1 text-foreground-neutral transition-colors placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weak focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:shadow-drop-low focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:border-stroke-neutral-strong disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:border-stroke-neutral-weak disabled:bg-background-neutral-weak aria-invalid:border-stroke-error aria-invalid:text-foreground-error aria-invalid:focus-visible:border-stroke-error text-sm padding-btn-lg" disabled=""/> <!-- -->Sign up flow works</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" class="flex h-9 w-full rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral bg-background-default px-3 py-1 text-foreground-neutral transition-colors placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weak focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:shadow-drop-low focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:border-stroke-neutral-strong disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:border-stroke-neutral-weak disabled:bg-background-neutral-weak aria-invalid:border-stroke-error aria-invalid:text-foreground-error aria-invalid:focus-visible:border-stroke-error text-sm padding-btn-lg" disabled=""/> <!-- -->Username claiming works</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" class="flex h-9 w-full rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral bg-background-default px-3 py-1 text-foreground-neutral transition-colors placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weak focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:shadow-drop-low focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:border-stroke-neutral-strong disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:border-stroke-neutral-weak disabled:bg-background-neutral-weak aria-invalid:border-stroke-error aria-invalid:text-foreground-error aria-invalid:focus-visible:border-stroke-error text-sm padding-btn-lg" disabled=""/> <!-- -->Adding/deleting links works</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" class="flex h-9 w-full rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral bg-background-default px-3 py-1 text-foreground-neutral transition-colors placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weak focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:shadow-drop-low focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:border-stroke-neutral-strong disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:border-stroke-neutral-weak disabled:bg-background-neutral-weak aria-invalid:border-stroke-error aria-invalid:text-foreground-error aria-invalid:focus-visible:border-stroke-error text-sm padding-btn-lg" disabled=""/> <!-- -->Public profile pages load correctly</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" class="flex h-9 w-full rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral bg-background-default px-3 py-1 text-foreground-neutral transition-colors placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weak focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:shadow-drop-low focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:border-stroke-neutral-strong disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:border-stroke-neutral-weak disabled:bg-background-neutral-weak aria-invalid:border-stroke-error aria-invalid:text-foreground-error aria-invalid:focus-visible:border-stroke-error text-sm padding-btn-lg" disabled=""/> <!-- -->Copy link copies the correct production URL</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" class="flex h-9 w-full rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral bg-background-default px-3 py-1 text-foreground-neutral transition-colors placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weak focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:shadow-drop-low focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:border-stroke-neutral-strong disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:placeholder:text-foreground-neutral-weaker disabled:border-stroke-neutral-weak disabled:bg-background-neutral-weak aria-invalid:border-stroke-error aria-invalid:text-foreground-error aria-invalid:focus-visible:border-stroke-error text-sm padding-btn-lg" disabled=""/> <!-- -->404 page displays for non-existent usernames</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Congratulations! Your Linktree clone is live! 🎉</strong></p>
